        +show: boolean
        +hide(): void

        -handleSubmit()
        -handleDelete()
    }
    class formDataReducer {
        +(state: FormData, action: FormDataAction): FormData
        -cases: NAME, EMAIL, BODY, PATTERN, REPEAT, TIME, ADD_TIME, REMOVE_TIME, ADD_WEEKDAY, REMOVE_WEEKDAY, PAUSE, LOAD_SCHEDULE, RESET
    }
    class FormData {
        +name
        +email
        +body
        +pattern
        +repeat
        +repeatMonth
        +time[]
        +weekday[]
        +onDay
        +weekNum
        +dateFrom
        +dateTo
        +paused
        +timezone
    }
    class EmailForm {
        +props: {email, body, dispatch}
        +renders email input
        +renders body textarea
    }
    class RepeatTimeForm {
        +props: {data, dispatch}
        +handleTimeChange(index, time)
        +handleAddTime()
        +handleRemoveTime(index)
    }
    class DaysCheckboxForm {
        +props: {data, dispatch}
        +handleCheckboxChange(e)
    }
    class getPatternDetails {
        +(data: FormData): EmailScheduleDetails
        -handles patterns: daily, weekly, monthly_day, monthly_weekday, yearly_day, yearly_weekday
    }
    class createSampleDateTimeGenerator {
        +(data: FormData): Generator<Moment|null>
        -yields sample moments based on pattern, repeat, times, weekdays, date range
    }
    class getSampleSchedule {
        +(data: FormData): string[]
        -consumes generator and returns up to 5 formatted samples
    }

        G[Date range inputs]
        H[Submit button]
        I[Delete button]
    end

    subgraph Reducer
        R1[RESET -> default state]
        R2[LOAD_SCHEDULE -> populate FormData]
        R3[NAME / EMAIL / BODY / PATTERN / REPEAT / ON_DAY / DATE_FROM / DATE_TO]
        R4[TIME / ADD_TIME / REMOVE_TIME]
        R5[ADD_WEEKDAY / REMOVE_WEEKDAY]
        R6[PAUSE]
    end

    A --> R1
    A -->|schedule provided| R2
    B --> R3
    C --> R3
    D --> R3
    E --> R4
    F --> R5
    G --> R3
    H --> J{validateScheduleForm}
    J -- invalid --> K[show error Alert]
    J -- valid --> L[getPatternDetails]
    L --> M[format requestData]
    M --> N{schedule exists?}
    N -- yes --> O[updateSchedule(item, schedule.id, requestData)]
    N -- no --> P[createSchedule(item, requestData)]

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
    participant User
    participant Modal as EmailScheduleModal
    participant Reducer as formDataReducer
    participant Validator as validateScheduleForm
    participant API as useEmailSchedule

    User->>Modal: open(show=true, schedule?)
    Modal->>Reducer: dispatch(LOAD_SCHEDULE or RESET)
    User->>Modal: fill inputs / change times / weekdays
    Modal->>Reducer: dispatch(actions...)
    User->>Modal: click Submit
    Modal->>Validator: validateScheduleForm(data)
    Validator-->>Modal: {error?}
    alt error
        Modal->>Modal: show Alert with errorText
    else valid
        Modal->>Modal: requestData = assemble payload
        Modal->>API: createSchedule or updateSchedule
        API-->>Modal: success or error
        alt success
            Modal->>Reducer: dispatch(RESET)
            Modal->>User: hide()
        else error
            Modal->>Modal: show error Alert
        end
    end
```

## Diagram 4

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> Idle
    Idle --> Editing : open modal
    Editing --> Validating : submit
    Validating --> Error : invalid form
    Validating --> Submitting : valid form
    Submitting --> Success : API success
    Submitting --> Error : API error
    Error --> Editing : user fixes
    Success --> Idle : modal closed
```
